shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_black_monday
	icon = GFX_goal_HOL_black_monday
	x = 0
	y = 0
	
	
	cost = 4
	available = { has_idea = rus_black_monday }
	bypass = {
		has_idea = rus_black_monday
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_idea = RUS_civil_war_aftermath_idea
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
	add_political_power = 25
	}
}

			}

			}
		}

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_currency
	icon = GFX_focus_rus_ruble
	cost = 4   
	prerequisite = { 
		focus = RUS_Nationalize_German_Assets
		focus = RUS_taxes
	}
	relative_position_id = RUS_black_monday
	x = 0
	y = 3
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
	}
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_KER
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = russia_must_wait_unlock
				has_country_flag = unlock_economy
			}
		}
	}
	bypass = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_idea = RUS_civil_war_aftermath_idea
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		add_stability = 0.025
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Nationalize_German_Assets
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_2
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_4
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_taxes
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_2
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_4
				}
			}
		}
		else = {		
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_Balance_The_Budget_tooltip
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_3
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_2
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_3
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_5
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_2
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_4
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	}

		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 248 decision = RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State } #Yaroslavl
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 252 decision = RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State } #Nizhny Novgorod
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 250 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 224 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_Local_Development_tooltip

			limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_6 }

	}

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_russian_army
	icon = GFX_goal_RUS_army
	x = 11
	y = 0
	
	cost = 1
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = russia_must_wait_unlock
			has_country_flag = unlock_military
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				psr_in_power = yes
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Alexandr Kerensky"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_The_Land_Quotas_Bill
				has_completed_focus = RUS_soc_land
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				rsdrp_in_power = yes 
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_vi_congress_moderates
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_vi_congress_internationalists
					has_country_flag = RUS_decided_to_stay_democratic
				}
			}
		}
		RUS_focus_blocked_for_non_decided_socialists = yes
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 90
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_russian_army"
		add_stability = 0.075
		army_experience = 50
		country_event = russia.54
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = rusd.48 days = 40 }
		}
	}
		
}
shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_Reintroduce_Okhranka
	icon = GFX_RUS_Reintroduce_Okhrannoye_Otdeleniye
	relative_position_id = RUS_russian_army
	x = -3
	y = 1
	cost = 2
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = RUS_Okhranka_tooltip
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_Okhrannoye_Otdeleniye_locked }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				psr_in_power = yes
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Alexandr Kerensky"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_The_Land_Quotas_Bill
				has_completed_focus = RUS_soc_land
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				rsdrp_in_power = yes
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_vi_congress_moderates
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_vi_congress_internationalists
					has_country_flag = RUS_decided_to_stay_democratic
				}
			}
		}
		RUS_focus_blocked_for_non_decided_socialists = yes
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_Reintroduce_Okhranka"
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" }
			if = {
				limit = { has_intelligence_agency = no }
				create_intelligence_agency = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_army_department }
				}
				upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_army_department
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = 50
			}
			add_ideas = RUS_okhrannoye_otdeleniye_1_lar
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = rus_okhrana_focus
		}
	}
}

		}

		}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			date > 1937.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5

		modifier = {

		}
	}

			bonus = 1
			uses = 1
			category = computing_tech
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = RUS_okhrannoye_otdeleniye_2a_lar }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_okhrannoye_otdeleniye_2a_lar
					add_idea = RUS_okhrannoye_otdeleniye_3_lar
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_okhrannoye_otdeleniye_1_lar
					add_idea = RUS_okhrannoye_otdeleniye_2b_lar
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_okhrannoye_otdeleniye_2a }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_okhrannoye_otdeleniye_2a
				add_idea = RUS_okhrannoye_otdeleniye_3
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = rus_okhrana_focus
				add_idea = RUS_okhrannoye_otdeleniye_2b
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = RUS_Project_Kremlin
					bonus = 0.5
					uses = 1
					technology = atomic_research
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_breakthrough_progress = {
					specialization = specialization_nuclear
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {
				limit = {
					controls_province = 7350 #OTL Kurchatov
					810 = { #Semipalatinsk
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
						can_construct_building = nuclear_facility
					}
				}
				810 = { #Semipalatinsk
					add_building_construction = {
						type = nuclear_facility
						level = 1
						province = 7350 #OTL Kurchatov
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					prioritize = { 810 588 40 }
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						can_construct_building = nuclear_facility
					}
					construct_building_in_random_province = { nuclear_facility = 1 }
				}
			}
		country_event = rusd.122
	}

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_Navy_Modernisation
	icon = GFX_goal_RUS_navy
	x = 36
	y = 0
	
	cost = 5
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = russia_must_wait_unlock
			has_country_flag = unlock_military
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				psr_in_power = yes
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Alexandr Kerensky"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_The_Land_Quotas_Bill
				has_completed_focus = RUS_soc_land
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				rsdrp_in_power = yes 
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_vi_congress_moderates
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_vi_congress_internationalists
					has_country_flag = RUS_decided_to_stay_democratic
				}
			}
		}
		RUS_focus_blocked_for_non_decided_socialists = yes
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_Navy_Modernisation"
		navy_experience = 50
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = RUS_naval_rearmament
			days = 730
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_Modernise_The_Petrograd_Dockyards
	icon = GFX_RUS_Modernise_Petrograd_Dockyards
	available = {
		195 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
	}
	relative_position_id = RUS_Navy_Modernisation
	x = 1
	y = 1
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = {
		focus = RUS_Navy_Modernisation
	}
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = russia_must_wait_unlock
			has_country_flag = unlock_military
		}			
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_Modernise_The_Petrograd_Dockyards"
		195 = { #Petrograd
			if = {
				limit = { can_construct_building = naval_facility }
				add_building_construction = {
					type = naval_facility
					level = 1
					province = 6174 #Petrograd
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { extra_facility = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { free_building_slots = { building = dockyard size > 2 include_locked = yes } }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { free_building_slots = { building = dockyard size > 1 include_locked = yes } }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { extra_dockyards = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { free_building_slots = { building = dockyard size > 0 include_locked = yes } }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { extra_dockyards = 2 }
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { extra_dockyards = 3 }
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = naval_base
				level = 3
				province = 6174
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { extra_dockyards > 0 } }
			add_one_random_dockyard = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { extra_dockyards > 1 } }
			add_one_random_dockyard = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { extra_dockyards > 2 } }
			add_one_random_dockyard = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = extra_facility }
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					can_construct_building = naval_facility
				}
				construct_building_in_random_province = { naval_facility = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_war_with = GER
				}

					has_war_support > 0.15

			}
			increase_mobilisation = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
				OR = {
					has_war = yes
					has_war_support > 0.25
				}
			}
			increase_mobilisation = yes
		}
		unlock_decision_tooltip = RUS_Attack_Germany
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = LIT
				LIT = { is_subject = no }
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_Attack_Lithuania_tooltip
